	"fmt"
	"math"
)

	if math.Pow(3, 3) == 27 {
		fmt.Println("ok")
	}

  console.log('not ok');

package main

import "fmt"
func main() {
	if len("") > 0 {
		fmt.Println("not ok")
	} else if 0 > 0 {
		fmt.Println("not ok")
	} else if 0.0 > 0 {
		fmt.Println("not ok")
	} else if len([]int {}) > 0 {
		fmt.Println("not ok")
	} else if len(map[int]int {}) > 0 {
		fmt.Println("not ok")
	} else if len(map[int]struct{} {}) > 0 {
		fmt.Println("not ok")
	} else if false {
		fmt.Println("not ok")
	} else if false {
		fmt.Println("not ok")
	} else {
		fmt.Println("ok")
	}
}

## - Yield -

x = 10
y = 20
_old_x = x
x = y
y = _old_x
if x == 20 and y == 10:
    print('ok')


x = 10
y = 20
_old_x = x
x = y
y = _old_x
if x == 20 && y == 10
  puts 'ok'
end


var x = 10;
var y = 20;
var _old_x = x;
var x = y;
var y = _old_x;
if (x == 20 && y == 10) {
  console.log('ok');
} 

package main

import "fmt"
func main() {
	x := 10
	y := 20
	OldX := x
	x := y
	y := OldX
	if x == 20 && y == 10 {
		fmt.Println("ok")
	} 

}

package main

import "fmt"
type Barney struct {
	Status string
}

func newBarney() *Barney {
	return &Barney{"ok"}
}

func (this *Barney) HappyAndKnowsIt() *None {
	fmt.Println(this.status)
}

func main() {
	barney := newBarney()
	barney.HappyAndKnowsIt()
}
